### Edit - 2026-03-15 19:34:31 UTC [20:34:31 CEST]

  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/agents/wave-controller.ts",
  "old_string": "  private async checkSingleStepPause(stepName: string, isSubstep: boolean = false): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      if (!fs.existsSync(this.progressFile)) return;\n\n      let progress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.progressFile, 'utf8'));\n\n      // singleStepMode lives under config (state machine format) or top-level (legacy)\n      const singleStepEnabled = progress.config?.singleStepMode || progress.singleStepMode;\n      if (!singleStepEnabled) return;\n\n      // For sub-steps, only pause if stepIntoSubsteps is enabled\n      if (isSubstep) {\n        // Small delay to let any in-flight file writes complete\n        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 50));\n        try {\n          const freshProgress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.progressFile, 'utf8'));\n          const stepInto = freshProgress.config?.stepIntoSubsteps || freshProgress.stepIntoSubsteps;\n          if (!stepInto) {\n            log(`[WaveController] Single-step mode: Skipping sub-step '${stepName}' (stepIntoSubsteps=false)`, 'debug');\n            return;\n          }\n          progress = freshProgress;\n        } catch {\n          const stepInto = progress.config?.stepIntoSubsteps || progress.stepIntoSubsteps;\n          if (!stepInto) return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      log(`[WaveController] Single-step mode: Pausing after ${isSubstep ? 'sub-step' : 'step'} '${stepName}'`, 'info');\n\n      // Set paused state\n      progress.stepPaused = true;\n      progress.pausedAtStep = stepName;\n      progress.pausedAt = new Date().toISOString();\n      fs.writeFileSync(this.progressFile, JSON.stringify(progress, null, 2));\n    } catch (initError) {\n      log(`[WaveController] Single-step mode: File access failed, skipping pause: ${initError}`, 'warning');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Poll for resume signal\n    const pollIntervalMs = 500;\n    let lastLogTime = Date.now();\n    const logIntervalMs = 300_000; // 5 minutes\n\n    while (true) {\n      let currentProgress: Record<string, any>;\n      try {\n        currentProgress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.progressFile, 'utf8'));\n      } catch {\n        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, pollIntervalMs));\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      // Single-step mode disabled — resume freely\n      const stillEnabled = currentProgress.config?.singleStepMode || currentProgress.singleStepMode;\n      if (!stillEnabled) {\n        log('[WaveController] Single-step mode disabled, resuming workflow', 'info');\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // stepPaused cleared — user clicked advance\n      if (!currentProgress.stepPaused) {\n        log(`[WaveController] Single-step mode: Advancing from step '${stepName}'`, 'info');\n        return;\n      }\n\n      if (Date.now() - lastLogTime > logIntervalMs) {\n        log(`[WaveController] Single-step mode: Still paused at '${stepName}'...`, 'info');\n        lastLogTime = Date.now();\n      }\n\n      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, pollIntervalMs));\n    }\n  }",
  "new_string": "  private async checkSingleStepPause(stepName: string, isSubstep: boolean = false): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      if (!fs.existsSync(this.progressFile)) return;\n\n      let progress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.progressFile, 'utf8'));\n\n      // Read singleStepMode from BOTH config and top-level (either can be authoritative)\n      const configSSM = progress.config?.singleStepMode;\n      const topSSM = progress.singleStepMode;\n      const singleStepEnabled = configSSM || topSSM;\n      if (!singleStepEnabled) {\n        log(`[Step] SKIP '${stepName}' (singleStepMode off: config=${configSSM}, top=${topSSM})`, 'debug');\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // For sub-steps, only pause if stepIntoSubsteps is enabled\n      if (isSubstep) {\n        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 50));\n        try {\n          const freshProgress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.progressFile, 'utf8'));\n          const stepInto = freshProgress.config?.stepIntoSubsteps || freshProgress.stepIntoSubsteps;\n          if (!stepInto) {\n            log(`[Step] SKIP sub-step '${stepName}' (stepIntoSubsteps=false)`, 'debug');\n            return;\n          }\n          progress = freshProgress;\n        } catch {\n          const stepInto = progress.config?.stepIntoSubsteps || progress.stepIntoSubsteps;\n          if (!stepInto) return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      log(`[Step] PAUSE at ${isSubstep ? 'sub-step' : 'STEP'} '${stepName}' (singleStep=${singleStepEnabled}, stepInto=${progress.stepIntoSubsteps || progress.config?.stepIntoSubsteps})`, 'info');\n\n      // Set paused state\n      progress.stepPaused = true;\n      progress.pausedAtStep = stepName;\n      progress.pausedAt = new Date().toISOString();\n      fs.writeFileSync(this.progressFile, JSON.stringify(progress, null, 2));\n    } catch (initError) {\n      log(`[Step] File access failed at '${stepName}', skipping pause: ${initError}`, 'warning');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Poll for resume signal\n    const pollIntervalMs = 500;\n    let lastLogTime = Date.now();\n    const logIntervalMs = 30_000; // 30 seconds (was 5 min — too long for debugging)\n\n    while (true) {\n      let currentProgress: Record<string, any>;\n      try {\n        currentProgress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.progressFile, 'utf8'));\n      } catch {\n        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, pollIntervalMs));\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      // Single-step mode disabled — resume to continuous mode\n      const stillEnabled = currentProgress.config?.singleStepMode || currentProgress.singleStepMode;\n      if (!stillEnabled) {\n        log(`[Step] RESUME (continuous mode) — singleStepMode disabled while paused at '${stepName}'`, 'info');\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // stepPaused cleared — user clicked Step/Into\n      if (!currentProgress.stepPaused) {\n        const newStepInto = currentProgress.config?.stepIntoSubsteps || currentProgress.stepIntoSubsteps;\n        log(`[Step] ADVANCE from '${stepName}' (stepInto=${newStepInto})`, 'info');\n        return;\n      }\n\n      if (Date.now() - lastLogTime > logIntervalMs) {\n        log(`[Step] Still paused at '${stepName}' (stepPaused=${currentProgress.stepPaused}, singleStep=${stillEnabled})`, 'debug');\n        lastLogTime = Date.now();\n      }\n\n      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, pollIntervalMs));\n    }\n  }"
}
```

  "new_string": "  private async checkSingleStepPause(stepName: string, isSubstep: boolean = false): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      if (!fs.existsSync(this.progressFile)) return;\n\n      let progress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.progressFile, 'utf8'));\n\n      // Read singleStepMode from BOTH config and top-level (either can be authoritative)\n      const configSSM = progress.config?.singleStepMode;\n      const topSSM = progress.singleStepMode;\n      const singleStepEnabled = configSSM || topSSM;\n      if (!singleStepEnabled) {\n        log(`[Step] SKIP '${stepName}' (singleStepMode off: config=${configSSM}, top=${topSSM})`, 'debug');\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // For sub-steps, only pause if stepIntoSubsteps is enabled\n      if (isSubstep) {\n        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 50));\n        try {\n          const freshProgress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.progressFile, 'utf8'));\n          const stepInto = freshProgress.config?.stepIntoSubsteps || freshProgress.stepIntoSubsteps;\n          if (!stepInto) {\n            log(`[Step] SKIP sub-step '${stepName}' (stepIntoSubsteps=false)`, 'debug');\n            return;\n          }\n          progress = freshProgress;\n        } catch {\n          const stepInto = progress.config?.stepIntoSubsteps || progress.stepIntoSubsteps;\n          if (!stepInto) return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      log(`[Step] PAUSE at ${isSubstep ? {
  "file_path": "/tmp/pw-scripts/wf-control-test.js",
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env node\n/**\n * WF Control Test: Tests single-step, step-into, step-over, continuous mode transitions.\n * Verifies all control modes work correctly with comprehensive logging.\n *\n * Usage: node wf-control-test.js\n * Prereq: Docker rebuilt with latest code, no active workflow\n */\n\nconst fs = require('fs');\n\nconst PROGRESS_FILE = '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.data/workflow-progress.json';\nconst API_BASE = 'http://localhost:3033';\nconst log = (...args) => process.stderr.write(`[TEST] ${args.join(' ')}\\n`);\n\nfunction readProgress() {\n  try { return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, 'utf8')); }\n  catch { return null; }\n}\n\nfunction sleep(ms) { return new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, ms)); }\n\nasync function waitForPause(timeout = 30000) {\n  const start = Date.now();\n  while (Date.now() - start < timeout) {\n    const p = readProgress();\n    if (!p) { await sleep(300); continue; }\n    if (p.status === 'completed' || p.status === 'failed' || p.status === 'cancelled') {\n      return { status: p.status, step: p.pausedAtStep || 'DONE' };\n    }\n    if (p.stepPaused && p.pausedAtStep) {\n      return { status: 'paused', step: p.pausedAtStep };\n    }\n    await sleep(300);\n  }\n  return { status: 'timeout', step: 'TIMEOUT' };\n}\n\nasync function waitForStep(expectedStep, timeout = 15000) {\n  const start = Date.now();\n  while (Date.now() - start < timeout) {\n    const p = readProgress();\n    if (p && p.stepPaused && p.pausedAtStep === expectedStep) {\n      return { status: 'paused', step: expectedStep };\n    }\n    if (p && (p.status === 'completed' || p.status === 'failed')) {\n      return { status: p.status, step: p.pausedAtStep || 'DONE' };\n    }\n    await sleep(200);\n  }\n  const p = readProgress();\n  return { status: 'wrong_step', step: p?.pausedAtStep || 'unknown', expected: expectedStep };\n}\n\nfunction advanceStep() {\n  const p = readProgress();\n  if (!p) return;\n  p.stepPaused = false;\n  fs.writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(p, null, 2));\n}\n\nfunction advanceStepOver() {\n  const p = readProgress();\n  if (!p) return;\n  p.stepPaused = false;\n  p.stepIntoSubsteps = false;\n  if (p.config) p.config.stepIntoSubsteps = false;\n  fs.writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(p, null, 2));\n}\n\nfunction advanceStepInto() {\n  const p = readProgress();\n  if (!p) return;\n  p.stepPaused = false;\n  p.stepIntoSubsteps = true;\n  if (p.config) p.config.stepIntoSubsteps = true;\n  fs.writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(p, null, 2));\n}\n\nfunction disableSingleStep() {\n  const p = readProgress();\n  if (!p) return;\n  p.singleStepMode = false;\n  p.stepPaused = false;\n  p.pausedAtStep = null;\n  if (p.config) p.config.singleStepMode = false;\n  fs.writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(p, null, 2));\n}\n\nfunction enableSingleStep() {\n  const p = readProgress();\n  if (!p) return;\n  p.singleStepMode = true;\n  if (p.config) p.config.singleStepMode = true;\n  fs.writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(p, null, 2));\n}\n\nasync function apiPost(path, body = {}) {\n  const resp = await fetch(`${API_BASE}${path}`, {\n    method: 'POST',\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n    body: JSON.stringify(body),\n  });\n  return resp.json();\n}\n\nlet passed = 0;\nlet failed = 0;\n\nfunction assert(condition, msg) {\n  if (condition) {\n    log(`  PASS: ${msg}`);\n    passed++;\n  } else {\n    log(`  FAIL: ${msg}`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n}\n\nasync function main() {\n  log('=== WF Control Test Suite ===\\n');\n\n  // Cancel any existing workflow\n  await apiPost('/api/ukb/cancel');\n  await sleep(2000);\n\n  // Start fresh debug workflow\n  log('Starting debug workflow...');\n  await apiPost('/api/ukb/mock-llm', { enabled: true });\n  await apiPost('/api/ukb/single-step-mode', { enabled: true });\n\n  // Start via the MCP tool equivalent (we'll do it via progress file manipulation)\n  // Actually, we need to use the MCP tool. Since we can't call it from here,\n  // we'll manipulate the progress file to simulate. But that won't start the actual workflow.\n  // Instead, let's use the REST cancel to ensure clean state, then expect the user to start it.\n\n  log('Waiting for workflow to be started (paused at first step)...');\n  const initial = await waitForPause(60000);\n  if (initial.status === 'timeout') {\n    log('ERROR: No workflow detected. Please start \"ukb full debug\" first.');\n    process.exit(1);\n  }\n  log(`Workflow paused at: ${initial.step}\\n`);\n\n  // === TEST 1: Basic Step (step-into mode) ===\n  log('--- TEST 1: Step-Into mode advances through sub-steps ---');\n  const p1 = readProgress();\n  assert(p1.stepIntoSubsteps === true || p1.config?.stepIntoSubsteps === true, 'stepIntoSubsteps is enabled');\n\n  advanceStepInto(); // Advance from wave1_init\n  const t1a = await waitForPause();\n  log(`  After step: paused at ${t1a.step}`);\n  assert(t1a.step === 'wave1_analyze', 'Pauses at wave1_analyze (next major step)');\n\n  advanceStepInto(); // Advance into wave1_analyze\n  const t1b = await waitForPause();\n  log(`  After step-into: paused at ${t1b.step}`);\n  assert(t1b.step === 'sem_data_prep', 'Steps into first sub-step sem_data_prep');\n\n  advanceStepInto();\n  const t1c = await waitForPause();\n  log(`  After step-into: paused at ${t1c.step}`);\n  assert(t1c.step === 'sem_llm_analysis', 'Steps to sem_llm_analysis');\n\n  // === TEST 2: Step-Over from within sub-steps ===\n  log('\\n--- TEST 2: Step-Over skips remaining sub-steps ---');\n  advanceStepOver(); // Should skip rest of sem_* and go to next major step\n  const t2 = await waitForPause(15000);\n  log(`  After step-over: paused at ${t2.step}`);\n  // Should skip sem_observation_gen, sem_entity_transform and land on wave1_qa\n  assert(t2.step === 'wave1_qa', 'Step-over skips remaining sub-steps, lands at wave1_qa');\n\n  // === TEST 3: Step-Into re-enables sub-step pausing ===\n  log('\\n--- TEST 3: Step-Into re-enables sub-step pausing ---');\n  advanceStepInto(); // Advance past wave1_qa, should enter classify\n  const t3a = await waitForPause();\n  log(`  After step-into from QA: paused at ${t3a.step}`);\n  // Should go to wave1_classify\n  assert(t3a.step === 'wave1_classify', 'Pauses at wave1_classify');\n\n  advanceStepInto();\n  const t3b = await waitForPause();\n  log(`  After step-into from classify: paused at ${t3b.step}`);\n  assert(t3b.step === 'onto_data_prep', 'Steps into classify sub-step onto_data_prep');\n\n  // Step-over the rest of classify sub-steps\n  advanceStepOver();\n  const t3c = await waitForPause(15000);\n  log(`  After step-over from classify sub: paused at ${t3c.step}`);\n  assert(t3c.step === 'wave1_persist', 'Step-over lands at wave1_persist');\n\n  // === TEST 4: Continuous mode (disable single-step) ===\n  log('\\n--- TEST 4: Disable single-step enters continuous mode ---');\n  disableSingleStep();\n  // Workflow should run freely. Wait a bit and check it's progressing.\n  await sleep(5000);\n  const t4 = readProgress();\n  log(`  After 5s continuous: status=${t4.status}, step=${t4.pausedAtStep || t4.currentStep || 'running'}`);\n  // Should have advanced past wave1_persist\n  assert(t4.pausedAtStep !== 'wave1_persist' || t4.status === 'completed', 'Workflow advanced past wave1_persist in continuous mode');\n\n  // === TEST 5: Re-enable single-step pauses at next step ===\n  log('\\n--- TEST 5: Re-enable single-step pauses at next step ---');\n  if (t4.status !== 'completed') {\n    enableSingleStep();\n    const t5 = await waitForPause(30000);\n    log(`  After re-enable: paused at ${t5.step}`);\n    assert(t5.status === 'paused', 'Workflow paused after re-enabling single-step');\n    assert(t5.step !== 'wave1_persist', 'Paused at a step AFTER wave1_persist');\n\n    // Let it finish\n    log('\\n  Letting workflow complete in continuous mode...');\n    disableSingleStep();\n  }\n\n  // Wait for completion\n  const finalTimeout = 120000;\n  const startWait = Date.now();\n  while (Date.now() - startWait < finalTimeout) {\n    const p = readProgress();\n    if (p && p.status === 'completed') break;\n    await sleep(1000);\n  }\n  const final = readProgress();\n  log(`\\nFinal status: ${final?.status}`);\n  assert(final?.status === 'completed', 'Workflow completed successfully');\n\n  // Summary\n  log(`\\n=== Results: ${passed} passed, ${failed} failed ===`);\n  process.exit(failed > 0 ? 1 : 0);\n}\n\nmain().catch(err => {\n  process.stderr.write('Fatal: ' + err.message + '\\n');\n  process.exit(1);\n});\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /tmp/pw-scripts/wf-control-test.js
```
